< Review>
The potato tacos are good. They taste fresh in a crisp fried tortilla she'll with potatoes, lettuce cheese and shredded carrots inside. Served with a side of rice and beans. Id come here again but nothing spectacular about them, as expected, which is good. The portions are large as the tacos themselves filled me up.  I didn't care much for the complimentary salsa that came with chips.

The service is quick and friendly; I came at lunch time and my food was out in less than five when the place was full.  They have bar seating which is nice if you're on your own for a meal.  There is also a nice sized outdoor patio if the weather is nice.

Needless to say the place is beach themed with a couple of TVs up.  The parking lot is small so street parking is the best option.</Review>

<Review>I live in one of their complexes in Siena Villas. It is so terribly ran lately. Sharing my review as my experience was so bad I’m leaving another review for FPI which is the parent company:

I've been living in Siena Villas for 5 years, since I move to CA. There's some great things and terrible things about it.

Tl;DR Verdict: Not worth it, looking to move out or find a house soon. Old amenities and poor front desk cancels out the good stuff.

The Good: Location and units.
It's right off of i-5 and between Laguna and Elk Grove Blvd, so getting on the road and heading out is super easy. I will miss this. The units overall have quite a bit of space as well, I feel like this could rival some condos out there in terms of space provided. I'm in a 2 bed 2 bath. It is also located near some incredible walks by the lakes nearby.

The Bad: Amenities.
The pool, gym, and amenities in the units all look great in the pictures. But I constantly had to open requests to maintenance on my dishwasher and microwave which they never replace, just patch up. The public amenities are by reservation due to Covid-19 which makes sense but when they were available, the grills and hot-tub would break all the time. One time they fixed the grill handle bars with towel racks and left them like that for a year. When you're paying $1,800 a month for RENT is this right?

The Awful: Front office. Inconsiderate neighbors.
The front desk staff is very forgetful and the managers are not very hands on. So be ready to be follow-up on your own issues because the office will not return calls in a timely manner.

They will take 3-4 weeks to respond to emails or important updates regarding lease but will expect a follow-up from you the same day when it's something they need, like payment.

When it's time to renew your lease they will give you ultimatums, either you pay the 20% increase for 8 months min, or leave in 30 days. Most recently I was trying to work out my lease with them in the middle of this pandemic and they were not punctual or helpful. 5 years, no late rent. Still got treated like I wasn't approved to live here.

Inconsiderate neighbors will let their dogs poop in public areas (like the little dog park) and not pick it up.

It is still a decent place, just be aware of what you're signing up for. I hope this was useful to you as a reader, and some feedback the office (or parent company) can work on.</Review><userid>108333934684574009988< /userid>< pics>

I’ve been living at The Courtyard Apartments for over 3 months now...Living here has been nothing other than perfect. Before we moved in, we even got to talk to a resident who’s already been living here for months, he said Yeri completely turned this place around since last management. She’s made Courtyard clean, SAFE and a home environment for everybody. You’d be silly to not move here or to not love Yeri! Her work dosent go unrecognized.

Updating...
Since the health concerns going on, I understand why the front office here at Courtyard @ Artisan Square remain closed, but I do not understand why the communication is so horrible and UNPROFESSIONAL. We have a new manager here, Yeri is no longer with us and it breaks my heart because I know if she was here, I wouldn’t be experiencing what I am. She got to know and familiarized herself with her residents and treated us as priorities, and made sure we were taken care of. I have called Brandy twice, who is apparently the regional manager of this complex. NO responses. I have reached out to Amy at Corporate. NO response. I am not one to ever complain, I love loving on people but this is just ridiculous. I should not have to call three managers to have my questions answered. If you all are working from home anyways, not sure how communicating or shooting an email is so difficult. The lack of professionalism, accountability and concern for their residents is disappointing. Rent somewhere who makes you feel like family, not an inconvience. <rate>1</rate><Review>I applied for an apartment in a new 55+ FPI project located in Englewood, CO. At that time, I was residing in New Mexico and was unable to handle the application process in person so it took nearly two months to finally receive their approval so I could schedule my move. This was by far the most convoluted application process I have ever experienced and I have rented apartments in several cities and have applied for and been approved for 2 VA mortgages, nothing compares to FPI’s application process.

I moved in at the end of December, 2016 while the building was still under construction. Immediately, I was able to see the lack of quality control and how cheap everything was. There was paint splattered on all the laminate floors, stains on the carpet and there were disgusting stains on the bottom of the toilet seat, all of which were reported to my contact person there. Keep in mind; I was the first occupant of this apartment. My monthly rent for my 2 bedroom apartment was $1,010 and it did include utilities.

My coffee maker tripped the circuit breaker at least once a week (I have owned this coffee maker for several years and lived in 2 different homes since this one and that has not happened). At one point, I worked for an appliance repair company so I am familiar with quality – all the appliances are bottom of the line junk. There is no sprayer for the kitchen sink and no garbage disposal. These are just a handful of issues.

This building attracts alcoholics, drug addicts and drug dealers, a few of the residents were molested by other residents. Homeless people are invited in by residents and once, a group of teenagers gained access to the theater room and were caught watching movies at 2:30 AM.  I was threatened by a resident while walking my dog alongside the building and another resident made a nasty remark about my dog.  With few exceptions, the residents are horrible. I feared for my safety. There was a constant stream of police called to the building, at least twice a week; I witnessed police cars in the entrance driveway.

Fortunately for me, I was able to move last month (September, 2017). I broke my lease, however, I was told that there is a waiting list for 2 bedroom apartments and my apartment would be leased this month (October, 2017). My final walk through occurred on 9/25/17 and I was told that I would have to pay for the carpet cleaning. This really upset me since the stains were reported within a couple of days of my moving in and I paid a $300 nonrefundable pet deposit. I called this past week to find out the status of my security deposit and if my apartment had been rented, I am still awaiting a response.

There was constant turnover of staff and a lot of drama. The person who was helping me rent my apartment quit last week.

The only positive remarks I can post are: 1) the location is very convenient, even though there is free underground parking; I was able to walk just about everywhere and 2) the maintenance requests were handled in a timely manner.

I would not recommend this place to anyone and judging by the FPI reviews posted on several websites, I am not the only who feels this way.</Review>< pictures>
